I watched it in OTT and it was an epic movie for me. These single-frame and wide-shot film genres will satisfy fans of Quentin Tarantino, as well as those who like to watch French and Italian art films. The first half ran well and smoothly, but  the second half slowed the movie down. LPJ developed a new Indian folk-western background score that conveys more levity throughout the film. I hope this movie becomes a cult classic in the future.

As a devoted fan of Mohanlal for the past 30 years, I couldn't help but feel disappointed with Malaikottai Vaaliban. While I've grown up watching and admiring his work, this movie left me less than entertained, and at times, I found it almost unwatchable. The movie-making and script, unfortunately, fell short of the high standards I've come to expect from Mohanlal's films. The storyline lacked coherence, and the execution left much to be desired. It pains me to say that my overall experience with Malaikottai Vaaliban was unsatisfying. Hoping for better projects in the future that truly showcase the brilliance of this legendary actor. ๐ฌ #MohanlalFan #HonestOpinion #MalaikottaiVaaliban

In my opinion, the movie was a remarkable experience. Drawing from my childhood filled with grandmother's folktales and festive theater, LJP's creation felt like a nostalgic yet innovative journey. Mohanlal's commitment to his role exceeded my expectations, and the cinematography added another layer of brilliance to the film. It was truly captivating.

Great trailer! Btw, It seems like it has become a routine habit for Mammu's fans and his PR team to start degrading Lal's films even before they are being released. I don't think any other Indian superstar has ever faced this kind of unjust backlash and toxic trolling from the mediocre public. Even though those stars also do have a share of their own "haters", they never get any kind of hate comments in any movie trailers of theirs.   It's really pathetic to know that we so-called "literate" Mallus are the only ones who do this thing. Lal doesn't deserve any of this! Maybe these people should think over the fact about how much an actor like Mr. Lal has done for our industry and films. Mammootty as an actor has never really reached these heights and achievements till date, no matter what these so-called fans say so.
